***стихия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стихия.html>стихи́я</a> (6262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στοιχεῖον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stoikheîon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихия.html>стихи́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stixíja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихия.html>стихи́и</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихия.html>стихи́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихия.html>стихи́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>element (one of the four classical elements of Ancient Greek philosophy)</li>
<li>elemental force of nature, and their spheres of influence</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> force of societal life that does not succumb to control by people or society</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> one's familiar, comfortable, or usual surroundings</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стихийность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stixijnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихийный.html>стихи́йный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stixíjnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихийный.html>стихи́йно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stixíjno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ти́хнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tíxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***стлаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стлаться.html>стла́ться</a> (18566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стла́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stlátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стлаться.html>стла́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stlátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spread, to spread out, to sprawl</li>
<li>to lie on the ground</li>
<li>to creep <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a plant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to speed over a surface <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of animals and birds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prepare for bed
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">постла́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postlátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стла́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stlátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sto</b> knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a <b>hundred</b> books</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стог.html>стог</a> (12269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stogъ</i>, from Proto-Indo-European <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stegʰ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thatch</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deck</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стог.html>стог</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stog</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стог.html>сто́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стог.html>стога́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стог.html>стого́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>haystack, stack, rick</li></ol>

***стоить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоить.html>сто́ить</a> (1505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоить.html>сто́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stóitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to cost
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больши́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto <b>stóit</b> bolʹšíx déneg.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <b>costs</b> a lot of money.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be worth</li>
<li>to be worthy of, to deserve
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1905</b>,  Фёдор Кузьмич Сологуб (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fyodor_Sologub" class="extiw" title="w:Fyodor Sologub">Fyodor Kuzmich Sologub</a>),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%91%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B3%D0%BE%D1%83%D1%85%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D0%B8%D0%BC%D1%8F_(%D0%A1%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B3%D1%83%D0%B1)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Благоуханное имя (Сологуб)"><a href = vnd.unilang:благоуханный.html>Благоуха́нное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a></a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Sweet-Scented_Name/The_Sweet-Scented_Name" class="extiw" title="s:The Sweet-Scented Name/The Sweet-Scented Name">The Sweet-Scented Name</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ишь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:благоуханный.html>благоуха́нное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>нехорошо́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маргарит.html>маргари́та</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>люде́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мени</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Ty <b>stóišʹ</b> tovó, štóby nosítʹ blagouxánnoje ímja, i nexorošó, što ty Margaríta, — no u ljudéj net dlja tebjá ímeni.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"You <b>deserve</b> to bear a sweet-scented name; it is not good that you are Margarita, but among humans there is no name for you."</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stóit tólʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative or infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ol><li>it is sufficient (for some purpose), all you have to do is, one need only
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1892</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" 7</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>Ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́дилось</a>, <a href = to ceiling was occupied by an enormous lump of iron, and that <b>if one could only</b> carry away all the iron, everything would become cheerful and <li>once (one thing happens another thing certainly happens)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1887</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9F%D0%BE%D1%87%D1%82%D0%B0_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Почта (Чехов)"><a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>По́чта</a></a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Post" class="extiw" title="s:The Post">The Post</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сентябрь.html>сентябре́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дные</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:взойти.html>взойти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнцу</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лода</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ло</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nóči v sentjabré xolódnyje, a <b>stóit tólʹko</b> vzojtí sólncu, i xóloda kak ne byválo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The nights in September are cold, but <b>once</b> the sun rises, it's as if the cold had never been.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1997</b>,  Андрей Юрьевич <a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>Курко́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrey_Kurkov" class="extiw" title="w:Andrey Kurkov">Andrey Yuryevich Kurkov</a>),  chapter 9, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>Добрый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ангел.html>а́нгел</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a></cite> |  translated as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrew_Bromfield" class="extiw" title="w:Andrew Bromfield">Andrew Bromfield</a>, transl., <cite>The Good Angel of Death</cite>, Vintage, 2009:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тика</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:строительный.html>строи́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новейший.html>нове́йшей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:история.html>исто́рии</a>, что́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:вроде.html>вро́де</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цемент.html>цеме́нта</a>. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:встрять.html>встрять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a>!</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Polítika — éto lišʹ stroítelʹnyj materiál novéjšej istórii, štó-to vróde ceménta. <b>Stóit tólʹko</b> vstrjatʹ v nejó — i vsjó!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Politics is only the building material of contemporary history, something like cement. <b>Once</b> you get stuck in it, you're finished!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not to be confused with most of the conjugation forms pertaining to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***стойка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стойка.html>стойка</a> (3212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stojati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stoh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стойка.html>сто́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стойка.html>сто́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стойка.html>сто́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стойка.html>сто́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stand (a device to hold something upright or aloft)</li>
<li>support</li>
<li>counter</li>
<li>stance</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стойкий.html>сто́йкий</a> (6041)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стойка.html>сто́йка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stójka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стойкий.html>сто́йкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stójkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сто́йче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>robust, sturdy, hardy, durable</li>
<li>stubborn, obstinate, resistant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stable</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stability</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resistance, durability</li></ol>

***сток.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сток.html>сток</a> (17782)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стечь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stečʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flow down, to drain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стек-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stek-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), with Indo-European <i>o</i>-vocalization characteristic of deverbal nouns.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сток.html>сток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сток.html>сто́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сток.html>сто́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сток.html>сто́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flow, flowing, drainage</li>
<li>drain, gutter, sewer</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a> (166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stolъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стола́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>table
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свеча́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столе́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svečá goréla na <b>stolé</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A candle was burning on <b>the table</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стола́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">so <b>stolá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">off <b>the table</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>board, fare, cuisine</li>
<li>department, section, office, bureau</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> throne</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столб</a> (2188)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stъlbъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">стлъба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stlŭba</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">summit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">stul̃bas</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">stulbs</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">stolpi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pillar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stolb</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столба́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столбы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столбо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>post, pole, pillar, column
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фонарный.html>фона́рный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столб</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">fonárnyj <b>stolb</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">lamp<b>post</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застыть.html>засты́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соляный.html>соляно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столб</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zastýtʹ kak soljanój <b>stolb</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to freeze as a <b>pillar</b> of salt</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***столбец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:столбец.html>столбе́ц</a> (17774)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stolb</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ц</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">léto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столетний.html>столе́тняя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stolétnjaja</b> žénščina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a woman <b>of one hundred</b>; a <b>hundred-year-old</b> woman</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***столица.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:столица.html>столи́ца</a> (1185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stolica</i>. Synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столица.html>столи́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stolíca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столица.html>столи́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столица.html>столи́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столица.html>столи́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>capital (city designated as such)</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столичный.html>столи́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stolíčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***столкнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:столкнуть.html>столкну́ть</a> (15917)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкнуть.html>толкну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tolknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столкнуть.html>столкну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stolknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкивать.html>ста́лкивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to push (off or away)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обстоятельство.html>обстоя́тельства</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:столкнуть.html>столкну́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obstojátelʹstva <b>stolknúli</b> ix</i> ― <span class="e-translation">circumstances brought them together</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cause to collide</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> table

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dinner

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столп.html>столп</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stolp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столп.html>столпа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столп.html>столпы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столп.html>столпо́в</a></b>)
</p>
